## Option 1: Quick Setup with Vite (Recommended)

1. Open your terminal in VS Code
2. Run these commands:
```bash
npm create vite@latest prompt-generator -- --template react
cd prompt-generator
npm install
```

3. Replace the contents of `src/App.jsx` with your downloaded file
4. Run the development server:
```bash
npm run dev
```

5. Open the URL shown in terminal (typically `http://localhost:5173`)

## Option 2: Browser-Based Testing (No Setup Required)

1. Go to [CodeSandbox](https://codesandbox.io/)
2. Create a new React sandbox
3. Paste your code into `App.js`
4. It will run immediately in the browser

3. Keep it simple and direct given their frustration levelThe backend-server.js file appears to have been deleted or moved. The file that existed when you ran ls -la earlier is now missing from your backend directory.

I need to provide you with the server code directly so you can recreate it. Run this command to create the server.js file:

```bash
cat > server.js << 'EOF'
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const app = express();

app.use(cors({
  origin: 'http://localhost:3000'
}));

app.use(express.json());

app.post('/api/anthropic', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { apiKey, ...requestBody } = req.body;
    
    const fetch = (await import('node-fetch')).default;
    const response = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'x-api-key': apiKey,
        'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01'
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody)
    });

    const data = await response.json();
    res.json(data);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
});

app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ status: 'OK' });
});

const PORT = 3001;
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`Backend running on http://localhost:${PORT}`);
});
EOF
```

Then start the server:

```bash
npm start
```

This creates a simplified backend server that handles the core API proxy functionality needed for your prompt generator to work.

3. Anthropic → responds back through the same chain

```
└── utils/               # Helpers
    └── cache.py
```

**State machine is brilliant** for managing:
- UI states (editing, generating, subdividing)

- Error states
